This book is bloodydamn brilliant. It's brutal and terrifying and complex and sO MANY PLOT TWISTS (!! even my reread still had me shook so there's that !!) that I just am going to sit here in awe of the author for a while. Okay? Okay. That puddle on their face is ME.<br/><br/>(holy shit it's all so very clever)<br/><br/><b>SMOL LIST OF THINGS I NOTICED WITH MY REREAD:</b><br/>• I remembered nothing before </span>
  <span id="freeText14667404889604566103" style="display:none"><b>REREAD #2:</b><br /><b>You know that feeling when you finish a freaking excellent book and your HEART IS JUST SO FULL?!?? </b>ME RIGHT NOW. This book is bloodydamn brilliant. It's brutal and terrifying and complex and sO MANY PLOT TWISTS (!! even my reread still had me shook so there's that !!) that I just am going to sit here in awe of the author for a while. Okay? Okay. That puddle on their face is ME.<br /><br />(holy shit it's all so very clever)<br /><br /><b>SMOL LIST OF THINGS I NOTICED WITH MY REREAD:</b><br />• I remembered nothing before this ah hhaaha whoops<br />• the audio is fantastic for me reading sci-fi...I understand so much better!<br />• EVERYONE IS A CONNIVING SLYTHERIN<br />• I LOVE THAT<br />• Seriously the finale scene blows my mind every time<br />• The world is so complex and the politics so intriguing and just...wow<br />• Cassius is precious and one big cupcake of honour<br />• Sevro is my actual favourite little shit and I love him and every time he opens his mouth there's 4 people lined up to say "NO SEVRO" which is beautiful<br />• Darrow...just Darrow &lt;3 &lt;3 He is unbreakable (although I admit I would've liked to see a little more of the effects of his torture?! Like mentally??? He bounced back rather fast)<br />• MUSTANG IS AWESOME I have so much more appreciation for her this time with how sneaky she is<br />• I hate the Jackal but he's also so freaking intriguing hahaha (im sorry)<br />• Sometimes my hEART STOPPED BEATING but I guess that's normal when reading<br />• time for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/33257757.Iron_Gold__Red_Rising___4_" title="Iron Gold (Red Rising, #4) by Pierce Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Iron Gold</a><br />• because stress! love it!<br /><br /><br /><b>READ #1: April 2016</b><br />Oh that was <i>good</i>. <b>That was really really good.</b> The ending actually made me feel SO ANXIOUS I NEARLY CURLED INTO A WITHERED BALL TO DIE. But it was <i>so so good</i>. And do you know how nervous I was about this book?! I've put it off for like 2 months! SILLY ME. (Actually, dude, <i>wise me</i>. I knew it'd be pain = and it <i>was</i>.)<br /><br />OKAY SO IT'S REALLY HARD TO REVIEW WITHOUT SPOILERS BUT <b>HERE IS A LIST OF MY THOUGHTS:</b> <br /><br />• This series is so very bloody. But Morning Star is like the bloodiest bloody that ever blooded.<br />• PLOT. TWISTS. PLOT. TWISTS.<br />• I still low-key ship Sevro and Darrow though. #sorrynotsorry<br />• I mean, THEY'RE FRIENDS. So.<br />• The plot was <i>super intense</i> with tons of battles and murder and revenge and war.<br />• Did I mention torture yet?<br />• THERE IS SO MUCH FREAKING TORTURE AND IT HURTS.<br />• Although I <i>have to admit</i>...the characters go through the WRINGER but I feel it's cheating that they just get a Carver to patch them up again all the time.<br />• Apparently "reinforced ribs" is a thing. <br />• I really struggled to like Mustang??? Sorry.<br />• Also is she named for the car or the horse? I GOTTA ASK THE TOUGH QUESTIONS.<br />• And I 100% confess <b>that a lot of the sci-fi techy talk went over my head.</b> This is a series I NEED to listen to on audio. I will absorb it so much better. But my puny eyeballs and weak brain reading? = nope. I struggled. I LOVED IT, but I felt lost and vaguely drowning most of the time. (I'm an auditory learning, so. Audiobooks and I have a re-reading date someday.)<br />• Sevro is my darling.<br />• Sevro is a filthy-tongued bloodthirsty idiot who likes peanutbutter chocolate bars AND HE IS MY FAVOURITTTTTTTE.<br />• I had <i>so many emotions</i> while reading. SO MANY. A book that makes emotions in the reader is AN EXCEPTIONALLY GOOD BOOK.<br />• I loved the ending.<br />• I need Pierce Brown's new series.<br />• halp halp halp I HAVE EMOTIONS AND MY VULCAN SOUL CAN'T HANDLE IT.<br />• I'm <i>happy</i> with the ending...but I AM ALSO A DERANGED PSYCHOTIC GRAPE OF FEELS AND SCREECHES SO YEAH. I DON'T EVEN KNOW.<br />• THIS REVIEW IS USELESS.<br />• *shrieks*<br />• READ THIS SERIES.<br /><br /><br />** QUOTES**<br /><br /><blockquote>The howling of wolves babbles from his helmet's speakers. It's Ares himself. My best friend in all the worlds has not forgotten me.</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>"Sevro." I lean forward. "Your eyes..."<br />He leans in close. "Do you like 'em." Buried in that squinting, sharp-angled face, his eyes are no longer that dirty shade of Gold, but are now as red as Martian soil. he pulls back his lids so I can better see. They're not contacts. And the right is no loner bionic.<br />"Bloodydamn. Did you get Carved?"<br />"By the best in the business. Do you like 'em?"<br />"They're bloodydamn marvellous. Fit you like a glove."<br />He punches his hands together. "Glad you said that. Cuz they're yours."<br />I blanch. "What?"<br />"They're yours."<br />"My what?"<br />"Your eyes!"<br />"My eyes..."<br />"Did yon Friendly Giant drop you on your head in the rescue? Mickey had your eyes in a cryobox at his joint in Yorkton -- creepy place, by the by -- when we raided it for supplies to bring back to Tinos to help the Rising. I figured you weren't usin' 'em, so..." He shrugs awkwardly. "So I asked if he'd put 'em in. You know. Bring us closer together. Something to remember you by. That's not so weird, right?"<br />"I told him it was odd," Ragnar says.<br />"Do you want the eyes back?" Sevro asks, suddenly worried. "I can give them back."<br />"No!" I say. "It's just I forgot how crazy you are."<br />"Oh." He laughs and slaps my shoulder. "Good. I thought it was something serious."</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>My chair rolls to a stop. his voice cut short, followed by a thump and sliding sound. My wheelchair rolls forward again. I look back and see Ragnar pushing it innocently along. Sevro isn't in the hallway behind us. I frown, wondering where he went, till he bursts out of a side passage.<br />"You! Troll!" Sevro shouts. "I'm a terrorist warlord! Stop throwing me. You made me drop my candy!" Sevro looks at the floor of the hallway. "Wait. Where is it? Dammit, Ragnar. Where is my peanut bar? You know how many people I had to kill to get that? Six! Six!" <br />Ragnar chews quietly above me, and though I'm probably mistaken, I think I see him smile.</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>"You tell anyone I cried, I'll find a dead fish, put it in a sock, hide it in your room, and let it putrefy."<br />"Fair enough."</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>"You and I keep looking for light in the darkness, expecting it to appear. But it already has." I touch his shoulder. "We're it, boyo. Broken and cracked and stupid as we are, we're the light, and we're spreading."</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="14667404889604566103" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1876119238" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1876119238" />
    <a title="Lady Luna. ✨" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/53385361-lady-luna"><img alt="Lady Luna. ✨" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1575639837p2/53385361.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1876119238?book_show_action=true">Jan 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Luna. ✨" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Luna. ✨" href="/user/show/53385361-lady-luna">Lady Luna. ✨</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/53385361-lady-luna?shelf=badassery">badassery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/53385361-lady-luna?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/53385361-lady-luna?shelf=great-books">great-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1876119238" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6289700744758180224"><b>4/5</b>★★★★<br/><br/> Buddy Read with team Howlers; <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/59458347-petrik' rel='nofollow noopener'>Speedy eye Oppa</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35431290-tweebs' rel='nofollow noopener'>Whorefart Aga</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7317186-celeste' rel='nofollow noopener'>Dewi</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes' rel='nofollow noopener'>Minxy</a> & <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35147071-jenn-the-dark-lord-scribe-house-of-slytheread' rel='nofollow noopener'>Voldemort</a> <br/><br/><b><i>“The Reaper has come. And he’s brought hell with him.” </i></b><br/><br/>After thinking on this book for a night I realize I have a lot to say about it, good and bad. <b>Read at your own risk because I'm about to bring the rant, minor spoilers may be included in this review</b>. So I thought Morning Star was a great conclusion to a fantastic series the Epilogue was gorgeous but <u>very short. </u> Let me start with saying I'm going to</span>
  <span id="freeText6289700744758180224" style="display:none"><b>4/5</b>★★★★<br><br> Buddy Read with team Howlers; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/59458347-petrik" rel="nofollow noopener">Speedy eye Oppa</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35431290-tweebs" rel="nofollow noopener">Whorefart Aga</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7317186-celeste" rel="nofollow noopener">Dewi</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes" rel="nofollow noopener">Minxy</a> &amp; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35147071-jenn-the-dark-lord-scribe-house-of-slytheread" rel="nofollow noopener">Voldemort</a> <br><br><b><i>“The Reaper has come. And he’s brought hell with him.” </i></b><br><br>After thinking on this book for a night I realize I have a lot to say about it, good and bad. <b>Read at your own risk because I'm about to bring the rant, minor spoilers may be included in this review</b>. So I thought Morning Star was a great conclusion to a fantastic series the Epilogue was gorgeous but <u>very short. </u> Let me start with saying I'm going to have <b>an unpopular opinion this time,</b> after completing Morning Star I am a little unsatisfied, I am left feeling like I need more and I'm kinda disappointed. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468159368ra/19673846.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>I personally felt like novel was too full of things that didn't matter, then the last part of the plot and the ending was great but so rushed. I feel like if Pierce Brown just published the last quarter only obviously less rushed, it would have been a more satisfying read for me. Don't get me wrong I really enjoyed reading this novel, I just can't help but feel like this whole book was fillers, and most of the story was unnecessary to the plot. Like this whole book was just basically talking <b>blah blah blah..</b> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1484558926ra/21729049.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>The plot was interesting and engaging enough sure, but there wasn't enough action this time around. So like I said if this book had have been the last quarter it would be on my favorite ever shelf next to Golden Son. This is probably even my least liked of the three, definitely the weakest (sorry). <b>But I'm not hating,</b>I did like this book, it just had a few issues that really stood out to me, especially after reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1875838159" rel="nofollow noopener">Edge of Bubbles</a> mini review on this book. Also for a whole entire series i kinda found alot of themes samey same as others, like the competition unoriginal, seriously Mars didn't even feel like Mars in book one it was so earthy, Space war also unoriginal. Really there was nothing new in this series, however this series does those 'stereotypical themes' justice, it is interesting, brutal, gorey, full of foul language and foulery (made up word) aka sack fungus. But still something new would be great. Pierce Brown has a funny sense of humor and it shows through his novels, he even managed to add a part into Morning Star that was a quote from one of my favorite movies Friday. The infamous "bye Felicia" &amp; he pulled it off, what a funny human being. :') <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1475145056ra/20686819.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><blockquote><i><b>“My name is Felicia au…” I feint a whip at her face. She brings her blade up, and Victra goes diagonal and impales her at the belly button. I finish her off with a neat decapitation. “Bye, Felicia.” Victra spits, turning to the last Praetorian.” </b></i></blockquote><br><br>I'm glad there is so many great things happening in the background to help relieve the brutally &amp; mind fuckery of the plot, I feel like if there wasn't a certain character (Sevro) I would have given this book three stars. Hang on a second this is meant to be the 'good' section and I'm still ranting! Okay let me try again. I loved watching the characters grow up together and grow as friends, it touched my black withered little heart. I also enjoyed the advanced technology in the story, pulse weapons, Moon Beams, Space Ships with AI. Pierce Brown also plays tricks on his reader by making them believe things that aren't true, I nearly hyperventilated a hundred times, like shit it was intense to read he also knows how to mind fuck you superbly, and make u cry like a baby. Im definitely a fan for life. It also opened my eyes and proved not all Space operas &amp; Dystopian books are not all terrible and im looking forward to looking into both genres more. <br><b>Reading the whole series in first person POV was shit. </b> I did feel frustrated at times with the first person POV however thats just me, I'm used/like reading multiple third person POV. So it did get overwhelming at times. Also this totally is not a YA, please do not assume that it is and buy it for your 12 year old kid, if you do they will be running around talking about sack fungus &amp; smelly balls while trying to chop each other to pieces with your garden tools. I loved the pace of all three books. Book two being my favorite of them all due to the brutalness and having an amazing ending. The plot is unpredictable &amp; full of twist. Some of the twists I did guess in advance. Cried at happy moments and sad moments, Pierce Brown definitely tells an emotional story. The writing is sensational. Overall a satisfactory series. It's great, it got my tick of approval and is now currently being worshipped by my <b>fan girl self.</b>I loved the twists towards the end of Morning Star, pretty impressed but not wowed, definitely looking forward to a Movie aswell as another series being released this year, apparently the new books are set ten years after the conclusion of Morning Star, so hopefully some questions I have will be answered in the new series.<br><br>So this book continues from the massive cliffhanger in Golden Son, these are not spoilers and actually mentioned on the blurb. Darrow is captured and tortured by the enemy, because it's Darrow and he is like a cockroach (ha) he escapes and continues planning his rebellion against the golds. Some old friends join him and others go against him, so it was interesting to see Darrow in the predicament of having to kill old friends to reach his ultimate goal. He also loses some of his greatest friends *sobs uncontrollably*. I thought this book had some fantastic &amp; rememberable moments. I am sad to say goodbye to the characters I have grown so fond of. Can't wait for the new series.<br><br>The character development was awesome throughout the series, we watched kids turn into adults. However I had an issue with Darrow the never dying cockroach. Is it just me or was Darrow a tad over the top arrogant, like I feel like I liked his character a lot less in this book. I also hated the fact that the whole book was Darrow making decisions etc like can someone else take charge for awhile? Like I get that his the captain, but <b>his always wrong.</b> I actually wish that something actually went according to plan in this book for a change. Also thinking about Darrow I have another issue, seriously like why does he let all bad guys get away with everything, friends who have in the past tried to kill him he happily welcomes back in his life with open arms. Like this quote made me think he turn back badass.<br><i><b>I am not alone. I am not his victim. So let him do his worst. I am the Reaper. I know how to suffer. I know the darkness.” </b></i><br>However he didn't. It was sad to see friends betray him but he is just dumb and naive. I did not like him having a conscious and mourning old friends aswell as friends turned traitor. It made me sad, so I hate him for it haha. <br><br>Sevro's personality in this book was my favorite of all three. Sevro went from a funny smart ass teen to a beautiful smart ass Adult. He was my favorite character and stayed consistent for me through all three books. I absolutely adored him and Adult Sevro (in book three) was my favorite. I love HIM. He has been welcomed into my ever growing harem of book boyfriends. Oh and I finally got my ship yay and predicted it from the beginning :). *howls at the moon*<br><br>Mustang is a wonderful character, I definitely had my ups and downs with her. But it's safe to say I absolutely adore her. I liked reading her development through this series, she is one character that grew the most on me. After book two I felt betrayed but it's okay now. <br><br>I also throughly enjoyed Victra she was another character who stood out, what a badass.<br><br>Ragnar was another perfect faultless character and another of my favorites from the series. <br><i>Hyrg la, Ragnar</i><br><br>A few of the friendships absolutely gave my heart a hard time, one being the bromance between Sevro and Darrow, towards the end of book three I realized I didn't actually like Darrow that much but instead was in love with his friendship with Sevro, all you folks out there know Sevro captured my heart in book one. I love them so much as friends, I love watching them grow together. One point in this book had me crying after they cried to each other. My number one ship forever is Sevorrow.<br><br><blockquote><b><i>“You tell anyone I cried, I’ll find a dead fish, put it in a sock, hide it in your room, and let it putrefy.” </i></b></blockquote><br><br>The friendship between Sevro, Ragnar and Darrow. Okay so this three way bromance was my favorite thing in the book (apart from Sevro) seriously the banter was good and they had fun together killing people. Seriously I love these three as friends. Especially Ragnar &amp; Sevro *heart eyes*<br><br><blockquote><b><i>"You! Troll!" Sevro shouts. "I'm a terrorist warlord! Stop throwing me. You made me drop my candy!" Sevro looks at the floor of the hallway. "Wait. Where is it? Dammit, Ragnar. Where is my peanut bar? You know how many people I had to kill to get that? Six! Six!" <br>Ragnar chews quietly above me, and though I'm probably mistaken, I think I see him smile.” </i></b></blockquote><br><br><b>Sorry but not sorry, one more thing that didn't sit well for me</b> was the big build up for Darrow wanting revenge, I feel like he didn't do himself justice, so the whole revenge thing kinda didn't happen.. How bloody dare Pierce Brown promise me revenge and blood without delivering it. <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1484561203ra/21729225.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Also the ending how they handled the worst villain ever was extremely disappointing, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ losing his tongue and dying by the noose wasn't enough in my opinion for the Jackal, he was an evil dog and made so many people suffer but Darrow once again let him off, he should have been a caged animal for everyone to torture and shit on until he ate himself to death. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> rant over.<br><br>I recommended this to everyone over 16, even if you don't like Sci-fi or fantasy this book is definitely a winner. I also feel like this book would be a great introduction to Sci-Fi. Please don't mind the fact that it is YA (once again I need to mention this shit) or in the kids section of your library, <b>this is not a kids story</b>. If my child read this book I would be so concerned it is full of violence, swearing, rape, cannibalism &amp; slavery. Hence the over 16. <br>If everyone's awesome reviews on this book aren't enough to convince you to read it, believe me when I say I'm even trying to get my husband to read it, because I know he will love it. Trust me on this he is a total book hater, I can't even get him to read a book if I read it out loud. (Lol maybe this is the reason why his a book hater?? I have an annoying high pitched voice). So go do yourself a favor and read it, it's <i>bloodydamn</i> good.<br><br><b>Whole Series rating: (totally stole this idea from Petrik)<br>13.5/15</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="6289700744758180224" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1085709793?book_show_action=true">Oct 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24685115-morning-star">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1085709793" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8537065089441920180">I'm not sure what I'm feeling right now. Overall, this is hands down one of the best trilogies ever. I don't think this final book was as good as the first two, but it is still a very good book and a nice conclusion. It's much more space opera like Golden Son than Lord of the Flies dystopian like Red Rising was. Lots of space battles, politics, and intrigue/betrayal.<br/><br/>I love this world and although I would NEVER want to live in it, there are some truly unforgettable characters. I grieve a little b</span>
  <span id="freeText8537065089441920180" style="display:none">I'm not sure what I'm feeling right now. Overall, this is hands down one of the best trilogies ever. I don't think this final book was as good as the first two, but it is still a very good book and a nice conclusion. It's much more space opera like Golden Son than Lord of the Flies dystopian like Red Rising was. Lots of space battles, politics, and intrigue/betrayal.<br><br>I love this world and although I would NEVER want to live in it, there are some truly unforgettable characters. I grieve a little bit knowing this is the end. There were a few times when I was really pissed at Pierce Brown while reading. I feel like he might have messed around with reader emotions a little bit too much. Reading this series is like reading/watching Game of Thrones - no one is safe.<br><br>There were some sections that felt overly long. A part of me feels like I should maybe give this 3 stars, but I just can't bare to rate down. I can't help it.<br><br>SPOILERS <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I was about to rage about Cassius and Sevro, but then they ended up being okay. I think I would have had to write a ragey review if things had gone differently with them. I'm a huge Cassius and Sevro fan. Still upset Ragnar died. I was iffy about Mustang for some reason. I thought she might be sketchy (was it just me?), but the ending surprised me. I didn't see that coming. I hated how things went down with Roque, but there was no redemption for him after Golden Son. So glad that Victra lived and survived. I lurv her. Some of the marriage and babies HEA stuff was inevitable.<br><br>ETA: Apparently, it isn't just me who felt weird about Mustang. Although I didn't have any issues with her past relationship with Cassius, I just never fully warmed to her again after Darrow revealed himself to her and she fled. I kept thinking she was going to betray Darrow or do something. She didn't. It was a typical HEA. <br><br>I feel like Cassius is one of the saddest, most romantic characters in the whole trilogy. I truly lurv him and am so happy he came around. *swoon*  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148164-buddies-books-and-baubles" rel="nofollow noopener">Buddies Books and Baubles</a>.<br><br><b>Original posts:</b><br><br>GAH! 28 page excerpt from Morning Star on Pierce's Facebook page today, December 8, 2015!!!!<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://redrisingbook.com/MORNINGSTAR3chapters.pdf">http://redrisingbook.com/MORNINGSTAR3...</a><br><br>I can't even.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449601991ra/17311144.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Update on Pierce Brown's Facebook page (July 23, 2015):</b><br><br><i><br>A little update for you all: the Morning Star first draft is complete, and I've been hard at work carving the second draft into being. This is my favorite part of the process, adding backstory, fleshing out character motivations, refining the plot arc to make sure it coincides with the internal arc of Darrow, and making my villains roar. <br><br>I love Red Rising and Golden son, but this is Mickey-Carved hybrid monstrosity. It's been daunting, but I'm proud of what it's becoming--the size of the world, the scope of the cast, the level of violence, the number of ships and moons and political parties...it's gonna be a fun one.<br><br>I can't tell you how excited I am for you to read it. Until then, I leave you with the immortal words of Sevro au Barca, "Shit escalates."<br></i><br><br>OMG OMG OMG #fangirling<br><br><b>THE PROLOGUE:</b><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.ew.com/article/2015/06/08/pierce-brown-morning-star-prologue">http://www.ew.com/article/2015/06/08/...</a><br><br><i>I got chills.</i><br><br>Just noticed 12/28/14: OMG, there is a title now?!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419823576ra/13135191.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Take your time, Pierce Brown, take your time. But not too much time.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418088146ra/12665722.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Meanwhile, I'll be doing a re-read and fangirling over here.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418088146ra/12665723.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7377305294245364831">So I'm halfway through this thing and I realize...I'm <i>not</i> going to survive it if Sevro dies.<br/>I <i>might</i> be able to handle it if Darrow takes a dirt nap, but if Brown kills off that crazy little Howler, I'll probably set my library book on fire.<br/><i>What? You didn't think I'd set something I <b>paid</b> for on fire did you?!<br/>Pffft. You obviously don't understand the depths of my frugal...ness? Frugality? <br/>What's a word for <b>cheap</b> that doesn't sound quite as awful? Anyone?</i><br/>Forget it. The point is, somewhere along the</span>
  <span id="freeText7377305294245364831" style="display:none">So I'm halfway through this thing and I realize...I'm <i>not</i> going to survive it if Sevro dies.<br>I <i>might</i> be able to handle it if Darrow takes a dirt nap, but if Brown kills off that crazy little Howler, I'll probably set my library book on fire.<br><i>What? You didn't think I'd set something I <b>paid</b> for on fire did you?!<br>Pffft. You obviously don't understand the depths of my frugal...ness? Frugality? <br>What's a word for <b>cheap</b> that doesn't sound quite as awful? Anyone?</i><br>Forget it. The point is, somewhere along the line, I started to realize that <b>THIS</b> was the last book in this trilogy. This<i> trilogy</i> that I'd easily rank as one of my favorites of ALL TIME.<br>And..<b>oh shit!</b>...what if it doesn't go the way I want it to?!<br><b>It was a sobering thought.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457023484ra/18310107.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was the first book that I've <b>EVER</b> actively tried to make last. Like, I would read a chapter...then go play Candy Crush on my phone till I screamed in frustration <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Come the hell on, you stupid fucking jellies! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>...then go back and savor another chapter.<br><br><b>Ok, so did I burn my 1st book?</b><br>Ha! No. I can't give you any hints without spoiling it. <br><i>Sorry...</i><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457024729ra/18310344.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I <i>will</i> say that I think this was a fantastic ending, and I'm glad that everything happened the way it...happened.<br>With the exception <i>one</i> <b>minor</b> scene.<br>Alright, now I don't think this is a spoiler, but for those of you who want to know NOTHING about what happens in this book...<b>WTF are you reading reviews for?!</b><br><br>K.<br>Now that <i>that's</i> settled.<br>So did anyone else think that scene where Mustang is telling Darrow that <i>It's not your fault</i> after <b>{name redacted}</b> dies, was janked straight out of Goodwill Hunting?<br>Like, word for word! <br><i>Psst...pretend Mustang is a middle aged guy with a beard for a minute.</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457026002ra/18310771.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457026002ra/18310772.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457026002ra/18310773.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>YES! EXACTLY LIKE THAT!</b><br>So, I couldn't really get into the emotion of the moment, because I kept seeing a young Matt Damon blubbering in his therapist's office.<br><i>shrugs</i><br>Whatcha gonna do? <br>Nothing, that's what! There's no such thing as a perfect book, but (to me) this trilogy comes damn near to it.<br><b>READ IT.</b><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1983313037" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1983313037" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577914102p2/3030788.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1983313037?book_show_action=true">Apr 26, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1983313037" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9927624812141885875">#1.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/882931268' rel='nofollow noopener'>Red Rising</a> ★★★<br/>#2.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1976416752' rel='nofollow noopener'>Golden Son</a> ★★★★<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The Reaper has come. And he’s brought hell with him.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>For those of you unfamiliar with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/882931268' rel='nofollow noopener'>Red Rising</a>, even though I might be the only one left at this point, in this world that takes place in our universe, starring a young man from Mars, everyone is subdivided into color categories based on their skill sets, income, hair color, and what last name they possess (information provided by <a href='http://red-rising.wikia.com/wiki/Color' rel='nofollow noopener'>the Red Rising Wiki page</a>):<br/><br/>➽ <u>
  <b>HighColors:</b>
</u><br/>•	<b>Golds</b> - Rulers of so</span>
  <span id="freeText9927624812141885875" style="display:none">#1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/882931268" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Rising</a> ★★★<br>#2.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1976416752" rel="nofollow noopener">Golden Son</a> ★★★★<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The Reaper has come. And he’s brought hell with him.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>For those of you unfamiliar with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/882931268" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Rising</a>, even though I might be the only one left at this point, in this world that takes place in our universe, starring a young man from Mars, everyone is subdivided into color categories based on their skill sets, income, hair color, and what last name they possess (information provided by <a href="http://red-rising.wikia.com/wiki/Color" rel="nofollow noopener">the Red Rising Wiki page</a>):<br><br>➽ <u>
  <b>HighColors:</b>
</u><br>•	<b>Golds</b> - Rulers of society<br>•	<b>Silvers</b> - Financiers and businessmen<br>•	<b>Whites</b> - The clergy<br>•	<b>Coppers</b> - Administrators, lawyers and bureaucrats<br>➽ <u>
  <b>MidColors:</b>
</u><br>•	<b>Blues</b> - Astronavigators of ships<br>•	<b>Yellows</b> - Doctors and scientists<br>•	<b>Greens</b> - Programmers and developers<br>•	<b>Violets</b> - The creative class such as artists<br>•	<b>Oranges</b> - Mechanics<br>•	<b>Grays</b> - Law-enforcement, security, military and other armed personnel<br>➽ <u>
  <b>LowColors:</b>
</u><br>•	<b>Browns</b> - Servants<br>•	<b>Obsidians</b> - "Monstrous race only bred for war"<br>•	<b>Pinks</b> - Pleasure slaves<br>•	<b>Reds</b> - The unskilled and menial laborers<br><br>Darrow, that young man that was born and raised in the mines of Mars as a Red, has some pretty traumatic things happen to him in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/882931268" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Rising</a> that has lead to him being the main tool in a rebellion for equality among the colors. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Justice isn’t about fixing the past, it’s about fixing the future. We’re not fighting for the dead. We’re fighting for the living. And for those who aren’t yet born.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I enjoyed this and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1976416752" rel="nofollow noopener">Golden Son</a> more than <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/882931268" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Rising</a>, and with the heartbreaking cliffhanger at the end of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1976416752" rel="nofollow noopener">Golden Son</a> I couldn't resist immediately picking up this conclusion novel. And I'm so very thankful I did, because this book was such an immersive and addicting read. <br><br>This being the final novel in this series, the rest of this review is going to contain <b>SPOILERS</b>. I'm not going to say exactly what happened, but you will obviously know who has lived and who has died, and you'll also have a pretty good idea about who was fighting for what side. Please do not continue on if you haven't read this series, or if you do not wish to be mildly spoiled. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“This is always how the story would end. Not with your screams. Not with your rage. But with your silence.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469402277ra/19814096.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That ending. That freakin' ending. That ending was everything. Like, my crops are watered, my family is fed, and my skin is clear perfection. I don't think I'll ever get over this ending.<br><br>Okay, so the middle of this book was very slow for me. Not that I don't love and have a soft spot for the Obsidians, and I know that story line was important to the end, but I was forcing myself to keep reading. I was pretty convinced I was going to give this a not so great rating, but that ending happened, that ending was everything. <br><br>I was crying over Cassius, because he is my favorite character, and absolutely hating Sevro. Then I was crying over what a perfect little cinnamon roll Sevro is. Then I was crying over Sevro, and hating Cassius with everything that I am. Then I was crying over Cassius, and crying over Sevro, and just crying in general, because I was such an emotional mess. Like, my body and emotions couldn't handle the ending of this book. Then Mustang went and just flat out killed me. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425970036ra/13955606.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The ending of this book is honestly up there with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1537756588?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">The Hero of Ages</a> for me. This conclusion was a perfect way to end this trilogy, and I feel almost at a loss for words, because I honestly believe Pierce Brown wrapped this series up perfectly. <br><br>Even though the ending was perfect, and I loved the beginning where we get to see the consequences of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1976416752" rel="nofollow noopener">Golden Son's</a> cliffhanger, like I said above, I was extremely bored during the middle of this book. And even though I recognize the importance of that middle section, I still can't bring myself to give this five stars, even though that ending was everything I could ever wish for in a book and I simply cannot stop gushing or thinking about it.<br><br>I also want to mention that I still hate Roque and I absolutely hated the way Darrow was impacted by his death. Like, gross. Please stop.<br><br>I was also pretty upset with Ragnar's death. I gushed about him pretty hard in my <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1976416752" rel="nofollow noopener">Golden Son</a> review, and I just think his character deserved better. I know that this story is essentially about an intergalactic war that is ever approaching, and that it is unrealistic that everyone makes it out alive, but I just wish it wouldn't have been him.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Our lives mean so much more than the frail bodies that carry them.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>But besides the ending, I did love many other things about this book and series:<br>➽ I loved the obvious social issues this book touches upon that mirrors our society that the people we place in power today. Obviously it's not as drastic as the difference between Reds and Golds, but maybe one day it will be. Hell, 2017 has been pretty depressing so far. <br><br>➽I loved the constant reminder of how important friendships are. I also loved how this book actually portrays friendship, and how you will fight with your friends when you believe they are doing something that is wrong. That's real and good friendship; wanting that person to be the best that they can be and that sometimes means calling your friends out on things. Sevro and Darrow are friendship goals. <br><br>➽I loved the importance of Darrow constantly building his social network. The whole spectrum of colors won this war, not just Reds and Golds. It was so believable the way Darrow made more and more connections and more and more important people and leaders believed in him and his cause. It wasn't just a forced happy ending where everything works out (I'm looking at you <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1630234463?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">ACOWAR</a>), but it was a constant struggle and battle, which Darrow worked very hard to achieve. <br><br>➽I loved Cassius and Darrow's whiskey conversation. It honestly gave me life.<br><br>➽I loved Quicksilver. Like, everything about him. Everything.<br><br>➽I loved the cannibals from the ship crash. It was so scary and atmospheric; I was on the edge of my seat constantly. Which probably also helped to make the part right after the cannibals boring.<br><br>➽I loved the realistic villains in this story, and even though they were horrible people, they were amazingly written characters who were all very believable reasoning for their actions. Also, the Jackal wearing that rib-cage broke me. Such a convincing and utterly downright scary villain. <br><br>➽I loved Mustang/Virginia and her character growth since <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/882931268" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Rising</a>. I know a lot of people have problems with her manipulating Cassius and keeping a big secret from Darrow, but this is a time of war and she has had to watch every man she has ever loved be evil. I totally get her not trusting anyone and doing some shady things to win a war. I'm not saying it is right or ethical, but it is believable. My heart bleeds for her character and what she had to watch her family become. I weep for everything she has given up in the face of justice, equality, and love. I feel like Pierce Brown wrote such a spectacular female character that is strong yet compassionate, beautiful yet brutal, merciful yet proactive, and so very real. She is one of my favorite characters of all time.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494290663i/22701329._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Breathtaking art by: <a href="http://gracezhu.artstation.com/projects/wBKrV" rel="nofollow noopener">Grace Zhu</a>)<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Life’s not just a matter of breathing, it’s a matter of being.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> I would completely recommend this series to anyone who has a love for SFF. I also have nothing but high hopes for the rest of Pierce Brown's career, and I cannot wait to read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1983258897" rel="nofollow noopener">Sons of Ares</a> this month and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1983315861" rel="nofollow noopener">Iron Gold</a> upon release next January. <br><br>And I want to give a huge thank you for all my friends that encouraged me to continue on with this series, when I was being very apprehensive over <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/882931268" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Rising</a>. And I want to give an extra special shout out to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/20712926-gelisvb" rel="nofollow noopener">Gelisvb</a> for letting me bounce all my feelings off of her, and for letting me gush and cry and rant nonstop to her. Seriously, she's amazing, please go friend request and/or follow her! 💖<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“They call me the Morning Star. That star by which griffin-riders and travelers navigate the wastes in the dark months of winter. The last star that disappears when daylight returns in the spring.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="9927624812141885875" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1542651294" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1542651294" />
    <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four"><img alt="Robin (Bridge Four)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473392517p2/14105531.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1542651294?book_show_action=true">Feb 09, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Robin (Bridge Four)" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four">Robin (Bridge Four)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781444759051" href="/book/show/26818907-morning-star">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=awesome-audio">awesome-audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=chick-i-want-to-hang-out-with">chick-i-want-to-hang-out-with</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=o-captain-my-captain">o-captain-my-captain</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=super-sidekicks">super-sidekicks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=kick-ass-heroines">kick-ass-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=want-to-throw-across-the-room">want-to-throw-across-the-room</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=book-boyfriend-material">book-boyfriend-material</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=fantastic-fantasy">fantastic-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1542651294" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8316613838241710139"><b>Braveheart in Space</b> is how I’ve heard Pierce Brown refer to this series and that is a good comparison. At some point during this series a favorite character will love, kill, die, betray, change for the better, change for the worse, make horrible decisions, make cold decision, sacrifice themselves or others, inspire, destroy, connive , manipulate <b>or frustrate you to the point you are ready to bloodydamn throw the book across the room.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455227463i/18076512.jpg' width='398' height='190' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The downtime and boring moments are few and far between and Mor</span>
  <span id="freeText8316613838241710139" style="display:none"><b>Braveheart in Space</b> is how I’ve heard Pierce Brown refer to this series and that is a good comparison. At some point during this series a favorite character will love, kill, die, betray, change for the better, change for the worse, make horrible decisions, make cold decision, sacrifice themselves or others, inspire, destroy, connive , manipulate <b>or frustrate you to the point you are ready to bloodydamn throw the book across the room.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455227463i/18076512.jpg" width="398" height="190" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The downtime and boring moments are few and far between and Morning Star tested my love for just about every character I was rooting for and made be despise to the very depths of my being the villains to our heroes. There is plenty of action to go around and it was an emotional journey.<br><br>Darrow is a hero with some reluctance and a lot of heart for a warrior. I am always amazed by his capacity to love and try and to redeem the people he cares for. He tries to give them all chances to break out of the cages of their culture and past to reach to be more and while I respect that greatly sometimes I really just wanted him to murder those who betrayed him. <br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I howl because I am a Helldiver of Lykos. I am the Reaper of Mars. And I have paid for access to this bunker with my flesh, all so I could come before Octavia, all so that I might either die with my friends or see our enemies brought to justice.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Darrow is a character I have always found easy to connect with on his journey. Had his wife not died he would never have left his little corner of the world. But now that he has he will never be that man again. In every book Darrow has grown and changed into something more than who he originally thought he could be. He becomes more and more complex and in Morning Star the dream he had Red Rising has to grow and change with him.<br><br>After being captured at the end of Golden Son, Darrow has been through so much and it has changed him. The first chapters are really rough as we learn what fate our hero suffered after the betrayals of Golden Son. They are harsh and have humbled him, they have also left him a little unsure of himself. When he actually makes it back to the war he finds that so much has happened in his absence. At first it is hard for him to find his place in this new war….but Darrow is the link that brings everyone together and he finds his voice and confidence eventually.<br><br><b>This is a wild ride.</b> I laughed, I cried, I cheered, I yelled at characters, I gave Servo a time out in the corner, I debated with friends over why I loved Mustang and they hated her but<b> I bloodydamn enjoyed every emotion filled moment of it. </b> <i>I’m pretty sure Pierce Brown is an immortal now being fed with all the tears and emotions of his readers.</i><br><br><b>
  <i>What I liked the best:</i>
</b><br><br>☭ <b>Darrow</b> - It is hard not to love a character who has been through so much. But the best part about Darrow is that he ALWAYS has hope and belief in the best of people. He is always sure that no matter their flaws they can be the best version of themselves if given the chance. <b> Except the Jackal because that dude is just cray-cray and deserves to die the death of a thousand paper cuts. </b> <br><br>Darrow is the embodiment of hope but his is not flawless. He doubts himself at times, he makes mistakes, he sacrifices, he cries more the Mustang and he is not without guilt. By the time the book was over he made some calls for ‘The greater good’ that were horrendous but he is our flawed hero and he really carries the story.<br><br>☭ <b>The Humor</b> - Remarkably for a book with so many brutal, bloody and heartwrenching moments there is the undercurrent of funny that softens so many blows. <br><blockquote>
  <i>” Do you like ’em?” <br>“They’re bloodydamn marvelous. Fit you like a glove.” <br>He punches his hands together. “Glad you said that. Cuz they’re yours.” <br>I blanch. “What?” “They’re yours.” <br>“My what?”<br><b> “Your eyes!”</b><br> “My eyes…” <br>“Did yon Friendly Giant drop you on your head in the rescue? Mickey had your eyes in a cryobox at his joint in Yorkton—creepy place, by the by—when we raided it for supplies to bring back to Tinos to help the Rising. I figured you weren’t usin’ ’em, so…” He shrugs awkwardly. “So I asked if he’d put ’em in. You know. Bring us closer together. Something to remember you by. That’s not so weird, right?” <br>“I told him it was odd,” Ragnar says. One of the girls is climbing his leg.<br><b> “Do you want the eyes back?” Sevro asks, suddenly worried. “I can give them back.” <br>“No!” I say. “It’s just I forgot how crazy you are.” </b><br>“Oh.” He laughs and slaps my shoulder. “Good. I thought it was something serious.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Sevro and Ragnar were hilarious playing off one another, but <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[seriously don’t open until after chapter 5<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Victra (YAY she is alive) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> is one of the funniest characters in the book.<br><br>☭ <b>The Side Characters</b> - Red Rising has some of my favorite side characters of all time. <b>Sevro and his wolf pack of one</b> is an amazingly fun character. We get to see a little bit of a darker side to him in Morning Star. It was always there I fear but with Darrow out of the picture for a while it took over his life. He made some really questionable, cruel and rash decision that I really wasn’t prepared for. I think I even put him in a time out in my head until Darrow could help straighten him out. I think Quicksilver said it best when they met.<br><blockquote>
  <i>“I did what I had to,” he says, sounding so small. “What no one else would.” <br>“Did you?” Quicksilver leans forward nastily. “Or did you do what you wanted to do? Because your feelings were hurt? Because you wanted to lash out?”</i>
</blockquote><br>He is still a favorite character of mine he just went a little off the deep end of power for a bit. <br><br><b>Ragnar became the heart in Darrow’s absence</b> and I love that stained to death. He became as loyal and good a friend to Darrow as anyone could be and even had some fatherly type advice and affection for him. <br><blockquote>
  <i>“A man thinks he can fly, but he is afraid to jump. A poor friend pushes him from behind.” He looks up at me. “A good friend jumps with.”</i>
</blockquote><br>He has come a long way from the slave he used to be and more than anyone has taken the term <i>”Break the Chains and live for more”</i> to heart and incorporated it into his life.<br><br><b>MUSTANG!!!</b> - I love her! But, in my reading group there was a great debate on her and her ethics/choices/morality etc. Is she manipulative? <i> Yes!</i> Is she cunning? <i>Totally.</i> Did she play the game better than some of the boys and make them cry? <i>Ab-SO-freaking-LuTe-LY</i> and I love her for it and I appreciate the PB didn’t make her some virginal Mary Sue who needed to be rescued. Virginia never needs a man to speak for her, rescue her or come to her defense. <b> Because she can do it all for herself.</b> I like that in Golden Son she was the one that used Cassius and not the other way around. I don’t care that she didn’t care about him at all. I’ve read plenty of books where a man gets to do that so I’m appreciative for the gender equality here. I also adore the fact that Darrow KNOWS exactly who she is and so he lets her come to her own defense and speak for herself. I appreciate that he doesn’t feel the great alpha need to defend her choices or virtues. He as always accepts the people around him for exactly who they are. And as for the big thing at the end….Darrow lied to her for years about being Red and she lied/omitted information to him for much less time. Even Stevens in my book.<br><br>There are many more…the Telemanuses, Orion, Holiday etc etc….but you get the jist.<br><br>☭ <b>The Action</b> - OMG there was so much of it and it was WOW….Close combat fighting, space opera battles, city revolts the list goes on and on. And every single battle seemed to matter, had something new and different to it and was never boring.<br><br>☭<b>The Villains</b> - There are many and I really couldn’t decide who I wanted to die more. At some point in time all of them were at the top of the list. First The Jackal, then Aja, then Cassius, Antonia, Roque so many horrible people that I wanted to die brutal deaths. The Jackal will be on my most hated character list for a long time I think.<br><blockquote>
  <i>“I listened to your proposal, now listen to mine. Run. Now. While you can. But know, wherever you go, wherever you hide, you cannot protect your friends. I’m going to kill them all and put you back in the darkness with their severed heads for company. There is no way out, Darrow. This I promise you.”</i>
</blockquote><br>☭<b>The Rip Roaring Race To the End</b> - Okay so the race to the end….I caught on pretty quick to what was happening but still that last 15% was nail-biting and I couldn’t read fast enough. But then at the end I was exhausted. <br><br><b>The Things I Had Issue With</b><br><br>Really there are only a few things and they aren’t deal breakers by any means. <br><br>There are a few instances where things go a bit over the top. Sevro for instance really stepped over a line with me. I still love the little guy but his character got really dark at one point and I really couldn’t believe that he very nearly killed one of my favorite characters. <br><br>Someone I loved died….(seriously not a spoiler guys lots of people have died in these books) I knew going into a PB book that it was probably bound to happen but I really didn’t want it to and WOW it was brutal. I cried, I had to put my book down and walk away and while sometimes I’m good with character deaths this one just racked me. Even the dialogue surrounding it tore me to shreds….<i>like I said PB probably immortal now from the tears shed</i>. I can’t complain too much because it fit in with the story and PB has killed at least one character I really cared about in every book. But alas I’m still upset hence in the issues section.<br><br>Other than that I’m not sure how I feel about the end. It is still really soon and I’m not entirely sure what I expected but it really wasn’t that ending. It isn’t bad mind you and you can’t tear down the entire society in a day it will take time. Maybe I just wanted to see something 10 years down the road to see how people are adjusting. The good news is that there will probably be some more stories in this world so I’m sure I’ll see some other types of closure there.<br><br><b>Overall</b><br><br>As overall Dystopian series go I think I only liked the Unwind series more (little less brutal). Everything was well thought out, characters are flawed and three dimensional and there is a great story behind it all.<br><br><b>Audio Note:</b> - The Audio for the entire series is fantastic. Tim Gerard Reynolds really brought this to life.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="8316613838241710139" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1082375767" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1082375767" />
    <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please"><img alt="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570038444p2/8422853.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1082375767?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please">Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=awesome-heroines">awesome-heroines</a>,
